                                            <div id="why-use-zillow" class="clearfix">
                                                <h6 class="zsg-subfooter-header">Why use Zillow?</h6>
                                                <p> Zillow helps you find the <a href="/minneapolis-mn/newest/" class="noroute"> newest Minneapolis real estate listings</a>. By analyzing information on thousands of <a href="/minneapolis-mn/houses/" class="noroute"> single family homes for sale in Minneapolis, Minnesota</a> and across the United States, we calculate home values (Zestimates) and the <a href="/minneapolis-mn/home-values/"> Zillow Home Value Price Index  for Minneapolis</a> proper, its neighborhoods and surrounding areas .  There are currently 187 for sale listings in <a href="/browse/homes/mn/hennepin-county/">Hennepin County MN zip codes</a>, including <a href="/minneapolis-mn/condos/" class="noroute"> condos</a>, <a href="/minneapolis-mn/bank-owned/" class="noroute"> bank owned homes</a>, <a href="/minneapolis-mn/short-sale/" class="noroute"> short sales</a>, <a href="/minneapolis-mn/rent-townhomes/" class="noroute"> townhomes</a>, <a href="/minneapolis-mn/duplex/" class="noroute"> duplexes</a>, <a href="/minneapolis-mn/land/" class="noroute"> land</a> and <a href="/minneapolis-mn/luxury-homes/" class="noroute"> luxury</a> listings.  If you're looking to<a href="/minneapolis-mn/apartments/" class="noroute"> rent in Minneapolis MN</a>, check out our extensive list of <a href="/minneapolis-mn/luxury-apartments/" class="noroute"> luxury apartments</a> and <a href="/minneapolis-mn/rent-townhomes/" class="noroute"> townhomes</a>. We make it easy to find your dream home by filtering home types, price and size. Filtering with keyword search is also possible, like <a href="/minneapolis-mn/waterfront/" class="noroute"> "waterfront" </a> or "<a href="/minneapolis-mn/on-main-lvl_att/" class="noroute">on main lvl</a>"  homes in Minneapolis. </p>

                                                    <p>The lender initiated foreclosure proceedings on these properties because the owner(s) were in default on their loan obligations. Pre-foreclosures also include properties for which a foreclosure auction is scheduled. These properties are not found on a multiple listing service (MLS).</p>
                                                </div>
                                            </li>
                                            <li id="pm-mmm" class="selected zsg-form-field">
                                                <input name="pm-mmm-input" id="pm-mmm-input" type="checkbox" class="checkbox"></input><label for="pm-mmm-input"> Make Me Move <span id="pm-mmm-resultCountWrapper"></span></label><a href="#mmm-tip-filters" class="zsg-tooltip-launch zsg-icon-circle-question"></a>
                                                <div class="zsg-tooltip" id="mmm-tip-filters">
                                                    <p>Homes with a Make Me Move<sup>&reg;</sup> price indicate the amount the owner(s) would be willing to sell for. They are exclusive to Zillow and a great way to learn about homes before they hit the market.</p>
                                                </div>
                                            </li>
                                        </ul>
                                    </li>
